		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus.inc.php');

	}

			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus.inc.php', $backup_name)) {

		}

	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('W1BsdWdpbl0NCm5hbWUgPSAiTXlTUUwgLyBNYXJpYURCIg0KYXV0aG9yID0gIlZpYVRoaW5rU29mdCINCnZlcnNpb24gPSAiIg0KZGVzY3JpcHRpb25IVE1MID0gIiINCg0KW1BIUF0NCnBsdWdpbmNsYXNzID0gIk9JRHBsdXNTcWxTbGFuZ1BsdWdpbk15U1FMIg0K'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode(''));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (!is_file('plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini');
	writefile_77();
	if (!is_file('plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini') != '3293eeb468fb3682a655a07afccacdb2c91526fe') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini') !== '3293eeb468fb3682a655a07afccacdb2c91526fe') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini') !== 'ab96924de2fd06afd1d43ce46354d96a1da63bde') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_77();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini') !== '3293eeb468fb3682a655a07afccacdb2c91526fe') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/sql_slang/mysql/manifest.ini');
		}
	}
}
